3a5(kha): dang / 'jigs khyed rgo ba sab sum rnams dang thabs tcig tu bzhugs'so// gnan yang rang rtogs dag pa'i 'khor dang / dgongs pa don gnas kyi 'kshir dang / rol pa tsho 'dul kyi 
3a6(kha): 'khor dang / 'bras bu rtser tshabs kyi 'khor dang / thugs rje 'gro 'dul gyi 'khor la sogs pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pas bskor nas bzhugs so// de yi tsho de yi dus na/ 'dus / 
3b1(kha): pa'i 'khor de rnams kyis/ sku gsung thugs mi zad rgyan gyi 'khor lo che ba'i yon tan brtsal med tsho 'dul gyi mchod pa chen po zhes bya ba ston pa la phul lo// de nas 
3b2(kha): 'khor de dag rnams kyi nang nas/ yi gnhen gtsug pud rang gi stan las langs te/ ston pa la/ bskor ba dang / lha phyag dang / me tog 'thor nas/ mdun du pus btsug thal mo 
3b3(kha): sbyar te/ gdng ba'i yid dang pro ba'i dbyangs kyis 'di skad ces zhus so// ston pa dri med rig pa'i lha/ smra bsam rang bzhin brdzod las 'das/ ma g.yos spros'bral lhun grub gter/ 
3b4(kha): yid bzhin thg med nyid la bstod/ e ma bon nyid spros dang bral/ thams cad 'dus pa'i ngo bo nyid/ 'khor 'das gnyis med rang dag dbyings/ gnas lugs mchog de bka' stsol / 
3b5(kha): zhig/ ces zhus so// de la ston pas bka' stsal pa/ nyon cig gtsug pud lha yi gnhen/ 'dus pa'i 'khor tshogs gus pas rton/ gzhi rtsa med pa'i bon nyid la/ tshig 
3b6(kha): gis mtshon du med na yang / ma 'ongs grol ba'i don phyir du/ yang dag nges par nga yis bshad/ ea ma ha/ cbon nyid rang dag 'dus ma byas/ gzhi rtsa med pa snying po'i don/ thig la 
4a1(kha): chen po gsung rung don/ thams cad kun gyi rang bzhin pa/ kha dag dbyibs dang mtshan ma med/ ngo bor ma grub stong pa'i dbyings/ yod dang med pa'i tshig las 'das/ 
4a2(kha): rtag chad mtha' las grol bar gnas/ skye med rnam dag con gyi dbyings/ bdag nyid kun gzhi byang chub sems/ 'chi med rang byung 'dzin med sems/ skye 'gag mtha' las 
4a3(kha): grol bar gnas/ snang la sna tshogs phyogs res med/ mtshan ma thams cad ye shes nyid/ rang byung ye shes 'dus ma byas/ snang stong mtha' la grol bar gnas/ rag pa'i rgyu 'bras 
4a4(kha): gang yang med/ 'dzin med rang byung ngo bo rtogs/ bsgrub med rtsol med bral ba'i ngang / dgag sgrub mtha' las grol bar gnas/ ji snyed ma spangs ji lthar dag/ ye shes rang snang ma 
4a5(kha): bcos pa/ bla med rang byung nyid la s+dzogs/ sangs pa'i mtha' las grol bar gnas/ thig le rang byung rang shar ba/ dman pa'i theg pa grol bar gnas/ rang byung spros bral bla med grub
4a6(kha): len pa'i mtha' las grol bar gnas/ zhen pa med pa rang byung ngang / gza' gtad med pa'i ngo bor rtogs/ yang dag rtsol bsgrub bral ba'i steng / gza' gtad mtha' las grol 
4b1(kha): bar gnas/ rang las byung ba'i snying po nyid/ khongs nas rtog pa med pa'i mchog/ rang las gzhan nas 'char ba med/ re dgs mtha' las grol bar gnas/ smra ba'i sgo mo tshig 
4b2(kha): mtha' yas/ yin min chig ga tha snyad kyis/ rang byungngo bo gting mi nyams/ sgro skur mtha' las grol bar gnas/ ye nas skyon bral kun tu bzang / ye zhes gud nas blang du 
4b3(kha): med/ zab mo'i dgongs pa mi g.yo ba/ blang dor mtha' las grol bar gnas/ thig mtha' med pa gsung dung sku/ ngo bo nyid las 'gyur ba med/ rgyu dang rkyen gyis mi 'jig pas/ 
4b4(kha): thig mtha' gnyis las grol bar gnas/ rang byung rnam dag grol ba nyid/ byas pa'i rgyu med bon gyi dbyings/ rtsal med rang shar 'bras bau s+dzogs/ rgyu 'bras mtha' las grol bar / 
4b5(kha): gnas/ lhun grub ngo bor bdag ma grub/ 'dzin pa'i yul med phyogs ris med/ zhen pa bag chags gting nas dag/ dge sdig mtha' las gril bar gnas/ 'khor 'das 
4b6(kha): gnyis med rangs zen/ snying po ye shes byang chub sems/ skyon dang yon tan mi 'byed pa/ 'khor 'das mtha' las grol bar gnas/ mkha' rgya cir yang rol pa las/ klong rgya / 
5a1(kha): gar yang 'gags pa med/ dbyengs rgya cer yang gting mnyams/ mkha' glong 'du 'phro dbyings nas son/ rang byung nyid las g.yo ba me/ ces gsungs 'o// nyon mongs / 
5a2(kha): rang grol ye shes 'khyel pa'i rgyud las/ gling gni yi le'u ste dang po'o// / de nas yi gzen 'tsho med gtsug pud kyis zhus pa/ e ma rang byung dag pa'i sku/ gni rtsa med pa'i 
5a3(kha): snying po las/ ma rig 'khrul tshul ci ltar lags/ ston pa'i phron mas bka' stsal 'tshal/ zhes zhus ston pas 'di skad gsungs/ nam mkha' gsal steng 'byur med las/ 
5a4(kha): sprin dang 'brungs s+dze ba g.yos/ tsha brang 'khrug pa'i tsho 'drul byung / de bzhin rang byung g.yo med sems/ nam mkha' ngangam rgya mtsho' grong / dmigs med bdal par gnas pa
5a5(kha): la/ sred bu'i bagnyal ma rig pa/ las dang nyon mongs bag chags rkyen/ phyi rol log 'khrul shes pa'i yul/ rgyu rkyen las dang yul bni 'khrul/ 'bras bu khams gsum 
5a6(kha): rgyu drug 'khor/ dper na rab rab mig bzhin du/ mkha' la gzha' tshan shra nad 'dzengs/ nam mkha' bal 'dab thags byu'i 'dzin/ ma rig log par 'khrul las byung / 
5b1(kha): yin min las la kun tu rtog/ bdag 'dzin 'khrul pa'i blo yais bslad/ 'dzin pa rang rgyud du mar rtog/ phyin ci log kun shes pa ltas/ gsum dang lnga dang drug dgu la/ brgyad 
5b2(kha): khri bzhi stong skye 'phel rgyas/ dper na ras la snam chen ltar/ spral gyis mi khog dbyes mi byed/ rgyu drug gnas su kha 'khor zhing / khams gsum 'khor ba'i rgya mtshor bying / 
5b3(kha): srid pa gsum du 'pho 'jug byed/ phyin ci log gi rgya ma du dam/ sdug bsngal 'khor ba'i tha rams bsdams/ bdag dang bdag gi 'dzin pa yis/ sna tshogs log 'khrul zhen par 
5b4(kha): spyod/ sdug bsngal tshe tshad 'dug tshul gnas/ snang ba'i yul la chags pas bcings/ skye rgas na 'chi chu bo bzhis/ chu gnyer rim bzhin zad dus med/ bag chags sgrib pa 
5b5(kha): 'thug pos non/ mun pa bzhis sgrib rig pa 'gegs/ 'khor ba'i las spyod grangs las 'das/ 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug dang / nga rgyal phrag dog khong khro yis/ shin tu 
5b6(kha): rgyal ba'i dregs pa can/ bdud dang srin po gnod sbyin bgegs/ sa bdag lha klu khyab 'jug tshogs/ dmu btsan 'tshams dang yi 'drig bgegs/ lha srin sde brgyad gdug tsub 
6a1(kha): kying / tshe 'drul mi dge n tshigs kan/ rang gi bbhla dang dpung du 'drul/ bhyen ci log tu tong pala/ mkha' glo dbyengs na thugs je skye/ gdul bya' dus la / 
6a2(kha): bb dus su/ gnyen po yi shes nang ba 'char/ zhes gsungs so// nyon mongs rang grol ye shes 'khyil pa'i rgyud las/ ma rig 'khrul tshul bstan pa'i le'u ste gnyes pa'o// 
6a3(kha): de nas ston pas bka' stsal pa/ 'khrul rtog 'djoms pa'i gnyen po na/ rang grol 'dzin med con dbyings las/ rang byung ye shes thugs rje shar/ dper na mun nag sgron me 
6a4(kha): ltar/ log 'khrul shes pa'i rgyu rkyen las/ yul gyi mun pa grol bar bya/ rgya chad phyogs lhung med par snyams/ snying po ye shes 'od zer las/ rang byung ye shes che ba'i rgyan/ 
6a5(kha): 'dzin med rang grol dag pa la/ dri med ye shes snying po nyid/ dngos med phyogs bral bon dbyings la/ skye ba med la sdzu 'phrul sku/ 'gags med nam mkha'i nyi ma shar/ phyi nang med 
6a6(kha): par 'od po che/ mtshan ma'i rnam rtog zil gyis gnon/ gsum dang lnga dang grangs med pa/ che ba'i yon tan mdzes pa'i rgyan/ sku gsum lhun grub dpe byad bzang / mtshan 
6b1(kha): dpe yon tan zad med mdzod/ mkhyen pa'i ye shes rtogs pa'i phrul/ thabs kyi rgyal po 'gro 'dul sku/ log rtog mtshan ma 'djoms pa'i dpung / skye med dbyings las longs 
6b2(kha): spyod rgyan/ spul sku grangs med bsam las 'das/ bsam gyis mi khyab brjod mi lang / ni rgyas dbang drag longs spyod du/ rigs dang sde tshan zhing khams bcas/ so sr spul zhing 
6b3(kha): gnyen por shar/ sgra bsam brjod dang bral ba las/ thugs kyi klong brdol pa rha'i lces/ brgyad khri bzhi stong bon gyi sgo/ rgyud lung man ngag bsam las 'das/ drang don nges don ston 
6b4(kha): pa'i bka'/ rang gsal theg pa rgyu yi bon/ bka' yi bye brag phun sum 'tshogs/ gang zag dad mos gnyen por shar/ rang byung ye shes thams cad mkhyen/ rnam rtog mi mnga' 
6b5(kha): dran rig thugs/ rgyu rkyen med pa'i snying po nyid/ ma bcos kun gzhi byang chub sems/ stong zhing bdag med bon gyi dbyings/ phyi nang kun gsal rtog pa med/ phyogs res med par 
6b6(kha): mnyam pa'i ngang / spyi dang rang gi mtshan nyid 'dzin/ bya brtsal med par grub pa'i las/ rang bzhin 'od gsal rnam par dag/ ye zhes 'od zer gsal ba'i mdangs/ ma sgrib ye shes 
7a1(kha): mkhyen pa'i mdzod/ dbang dang khyin brlabs dngos grub gter/ me rtog 'gro 'dul thabs las mkhas/ mrig dug 'dzoms gnyen par shar/ rang byung yon tan dun / 
7a2(kha): sum 'tshogs/ yid bzhin nor bu 'drul po che/ ye shes 'di zer che ba'i rgyan/ gser gyi nye ma rang byung sku/ 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i stobs po cha/ lhun grub yon tan rang dag 
7a3(kha): gsal/ legs pa kun 'byung thugs rje grub/ nam mkha'i dbyings dang rgya mtsho'i klong / nub pa med pa'i snying por bdag/ cho' yangs so yon tan mchog/ kun snyoms yon tan / 
7a4(kha): gnyen por shar/ khyab bdal lhun grub ye shes che/ mdzad spyod rnam dag phun sum tshogs/ bya bral rtsol sgrub bral ba'i sdeng / 'phren las mthar bhyin lhun gyis grub
7a5(kha): mdzad spyod thabs kyi ye shes kyis/ zhian chags med pa'i dbyings su pbyer/ kun grub 'phren las gnyen por shar/ zhes gsungs so// nyon mongs rang grol ye shes 'khyel pa'i rgyud 
7a6(kha): las/ gnyen po ye shes kyi gnas lugs bstan pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// // ston pa'i sgron mes bka' stsal pa/ dus gsum 'gyur med g.yung drung sems/ bskal par mi 
7b1(kha): thub rgyal mtshan can/ srid par 'khyams kyang sems mi ster/ 'byung ba 'khrug kyang yid mi shrebg/ dus gsum bral yang dbyings mi nyams/ stong gsum 'gyur yang klong mi 'ghyugs/ 
7b2(kha): thams gsum 'thab kyang mkha' ma bsreg/ rang gsala rang steng 'byur ba mid/ skad cig gcig la s+dzogs mnyam nyid/ rang gsal rang byung yo zhes nyed/ stong pa bon nyid dbyings du 
7b3(kha): grol/ de gsum mi byed gcig gisan/ mnyam nyid phyogs res med par gnas/ brtsal du med pa'i ye shes che/ 'du 'bral med par lhun gyis grub/ tag chad mtha' bral 
7b4(kha): chen por dag/ dag pa nyid kyang dag la gnas/ 'das pa'i bon la bshad du med/ dper na nam mkha'i igs dbyebs lthar/ mthun ni gang yang mthun pa la/ yin ni ci yang ma 
7b5(kha): yin pa/ 'char ni cer yang 'char ba la/ grub ni mtshan mar ma grub pa/ mthar ma ltung ba'i ye shes nyid/ 'phel 'grib med pa'i ngo bor gnas/ lta ba'i don gnas rangs zin/ 
7b6(kha): nyon mongs rang grol chen po yin/ ye zhes chen po'i glong chub nas/ dug lnga rang gi rtsa ba chod/ rnam rtog chu bran rka chad 'dra/ 'khor ba'i zhings dbyings su thim/ sred par mi 
8a1(kha): thub gsung dun sems/ phyogs su ma lbang lta ba'i gan/ gnhi rtsa med pa'i snying po la/ gzugs su ma grub mtshan ma med// dlung po byang sems men par shes/ sgra / 
8a2(kha): bsam brjod dang bral ba la/ dran rig mi 'khrul g.sung dru thugs/ che ba'i yon tan sprul pa'i rgyan/ rtsol sgrub med par spyod las 'das/ rang byung rig pa spye brug shar/ con 
8a3(kha): kun rtsa ba byang chub sems/ sems las ma gtogs bon rnams med/ sems nyid rtogs pa'i khyad par las/ che ba'i yon tan rtsal ma 'gags/ mya ngan 'das pa'i bon du 
8a4(kha): shar/ sems nyid ma rtogs 'khrul pa las/ log zhes cho 'phrul bsam mi khyab/ 'khor ba'i bon rnams sna tshogs shar/ sems nyid gsas mkhar ci lta ba/ mu bzhi gang du ma 
8a5(kha): grub la/ mu bzhi gang du ma 'gag pa'o// sems nyid gsas mkhar yod pa de/ yod na stong du ga la 'dod/ rnam par rtog pa 'gags pa men/ mya ngan 'da' ba gang zhig 'ong / 
8a6(kha): gzhig pas dngos po grol mi gyur/ sems nyid gsas mkhar med pa men/ med na rig pa ci ltar 'char/ rnam pa thams cad ci ltar mkhyen/ 'khor ba'i rgyu drug lhung mi bsrid// 
8b1(kha): thar pa'i 'bras bu lam mi rnyed/ sems nyid gsas mkhar gnyis ka men/ yin na gnyis su 'dres mi rung / rnam rtog mi mnga' cir yang gsal/ gsal la ma rtogs 'byung mi / 
8b2(kha): 'gyur/ sems nyid gsas mkhar gnyis med min/ yin na rtogs dang ma rtogs dang / 'khor ba mya ngan 'das pa dang / gnyen po nyon mongs 'byung mi 'gyur/ rang bzhin lhun grub 
8b3(kha): snying po nyid/ mkha' klong dbyings kyi gsas mkhar du / ci yang ma yin cir yang 'char/ ma grub ma 'gag gcig la s+dzogs/ zhen pa'i sgro 'dogs bskur 'debs med/ kun grol 
8b4(kha): gsas mkhar chen po ste/ thub pa med pa'i rgyal mtshan can/ dper na nam mkha'i khyung chen bzhin/ pyi rgya brlabs kyis chod par gnas/ mkha' la nyi m shar ba ltar/ 
8b5(kha): kun la gsal zhing snyoms par gnas/ rgya mtsho chen po'i klong yangs ltar/ phyi nang snod bcud s+dzogs par gnas/ zhes gsungs so// nyon mongs rang grol ye shes 'khyel pa'i rgyud 
8b6(kha): las/ lta ba rang grol bstan pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// // ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ g.yung drung yi kheb gsas mkhar la/ gar yang mi brtsal spyod pa kun las 
9a1(kha): 'das/ dmigs med mi g.yo rang sems ye thuab tu/ dbyings nas minyams klong nas mi g.yo zhing / mkha' la mi 'khrug cig le gcig tu bnag/ rig pa stong / 
9a2(kha): gsal 'gyur med dbyings nyid du / lus kyi bya byed ci bder bcos pa dang / byeng rgod dbugs nyid cha la dbab pa dang / yod kyi blon po byar btang byas nas/ shes pa phyi ya yul du rig pa 
9a3(kha): nang gi sems/ nam mkha' rang bzhin khyab bdal chen po ru/ ma yaings lhang lhan ner dgongs par gsal/ reig pa lhangs kyis gsal ba'i lhag mtsong la/ rig pa nges bzang 
9a4(kha): bral ba'i ni gnas mchog/ stong gsal dbyer med zung du 'brel ba'i bon/ ma yings ngang la gnas pa rtogs pa'i phul/ nga dang rang bzhin ma bcos bdag med par/ 'gyur med 
9a5(kha): dbyings su bzhag pa bon sku'i mchog/ mi g.yo dbyings la kun 'byung glrong 'khrug ste/ mkha' la log par snang ba'i rjzes 'breng nas/ rtogs pas nang bkang spyod pas phye bkang zhing / 
9a6(kha): 'dzin pas bdag bcings bzung bas gzhan bcings nas/ gsas mkhar g.sung drung sems kyi don mi gsal/ brtsol ba'i bya brtsal 'khrul pa'i dmag gseab tu/ dmyal ba'i / 
9b1(kha): gring bzung ngan song btsin du khrid/ thar pa'i lam bral byang chub sems dang 'gyang / khams gsum 'khor ba'i gnas nas grol mi 'gyur/ khams gsum 'khor ba gting nas spug 
9b2(kha): pa'i phyir/ g.sung drung y khyab gsas mkhar snying po ru/ gar sphyin rtsi la sbrang ma chags pa bzhin/ dbyings dang rig pa gnyis med gang la gnas/ ma yeng mi 'gyur don gsal lhun 
9b3(kha): gyis grub/ 'bras bu brtsal med rnam pa thams cad mkhyen/ rtog med rang grol chen po'i dbyings su bsgyur/ zhes gsungs so// nyon mongs rang grol ye zhes 'khyil pa'i rgyud 
9b4(kha): las/ dgongs pa rang grol bstan pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// / ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ lha dgongs gnyis med 'du 'bral med paru/ snang ba rang grol bhar ba spyod pa'i / 
9b5(kha): mchog/ lus mi thub pa 'dus ma byas pa'i sku/ ngag mi thrub pa brjod dang bral ba'i gsung / yid mi thrub pa bsam las 'das pa'i thugs/ mkha' grong dbyings su bdal khyab chen 
9b6(kha): po'i gnas/ spyod pa'i dgongs pa mdzad pa thugs rje tche/ ma lus mi phye blang dor med par snyom/ che chung bzangngan med par kun gsal dag/ gzung 'dzin 'khrul pa'i bon du nang 
10a1(kha): bkun/ rang bzhin nyid du 'jig dang 'gag par 'gyur/ btag tu mi bzod 'khor ba'i bon/ phyi ye 'jig rten rnod 'di dag/ rang bzhin 'dzin chags stong gnas 
10a2(kha): grol/ dbyar rgun ston dbyed dus bzhi yang / bzung du mi zen dgag mi khog/ rang bzhin 'byung zhing rang bzhin grol/ sems kyi 'gyu rtog yid kyi bon/ skad cig mi gnas dus 
10a3(kha): gsum 'gyur/ bzung bas mi zen dgag mi khog/ rang bzhin 'byung zhing rang bzhin grol/ rang grol chen po spyod pa'i mchog/ bde skyed longs spyed pun sum tshogs/ byams 
10a4(kha): sdug gnyen mtshan thams cad la/ zhen med rang grol spyod pa'i mchog/ tdug cing phongs pa mi khom yul/ dgra sdang rgol ba thams cad la/ sdang byed rang grol spyod pa'i mchog/ 
10a5(kha): byae dang nang gis bsdus pa'i bon/ sems dang sems las byung ba rnams/ rang byung ye shes dgongs pa las/ rang grol gzug ma'i spyod pa yi/ yengs med 'o thub rgyun la bzhag/ dper 
10a6(kha): na 'dam gyi p ro ltar/ nyes pa'i skyon bral yon tan s+dzogs/ gsas mkhar sgo gsum spyod pa 'di/ mzhen ma chags lhug par cing / thugs rje thabs kyis sprul pa yis/ 
10b1(kha): 'gro ba log 'khrul don la bzung / ye shes sprul pa'i spyod pa yis/ dgongs pa'i don gsal nyams su blangs/ byin brlabs nus pa'i spyod pa yis/ gdug cing sregs pa'i log / 
10b2(kha): rtog gnom/ mbthun 'jug thabs kyi spyod pa zad/ spyod pa'i bon nyid ma bcos pa/ dper na seng gi rtsal s+dzogs bzhin/ nyam g med par grol bar 'gyur/ zhes gsungs so// 
10b3(kha): nyon mongs rang grol ye shes 'khyel pa'i rgyud las/ spyod pa rang grol du bstan pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// // ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ 'bras bu brtsal med sangs rgyas / 
10b4(kha): dngos/ thub pa med pa'i rgyal mtshan can/ 'gyur ba med pa'i gsung drung sku/ 'du 'bral med pa'i byang chub sems/ thig mtha' med pa ye zshes can/ rang byung ye shes snying po nyid/ 
10b5(kha): rangs zen na 'bras bu'i mchog/ bya brtsal rtsol sgrub bral ba'i gding / mi rtog ye zhes dgongs pa'i thugs/ gsal stong 'gyur med lhun gyis grub/ mkha' gsal rangs 
10b6(kha): zin pa yi/ rnam pa thams cad cer yang mkhyen/ ma rig rmongs pa'i 'khrul pa sangs/ thugs rje ye shes dpag med shar/ mya ngan 'das pa'i mthar ma ltung / klong stong rangs zin / 
11a1(kha): / #/ pa yis/ ngdang bdag tu bzung ba grol/ dmigs pa'i mtha' rnams kun dang bral/ mi rtog ye shes rang byung shar/ bdal pa chen po kun la khyab/ 'khor ba'i mtha' 
11a2(kha): las 'das par gnas/ 'gyur med dbyings mnyams zien pa/ skye rgas na 'chi bzhi dang bral/ dus gsum 'gyur ba'i blo las grol/ mi nub g.sung drung rgyal mtshan can/ 'bras 
11a3(kha): bu bla med sangs rgyas ging / 'das pa'i bde bar ghegs pa yang / rang rigs zen mngon sangs rgyas/ da lta bzhugs pa'i bon gnhen kyang / rang rig gims pas 'bras bu tib/ slan 
11a4(kha): nas byen pa'i lha gnhen kyang / rang rig rtogs pa'i 'bras bu yin/ 'bras bu gzhan la re sa med/ rang gsal rtogs pas thams cad mkhyen/ rang stong rtogs pas bdag 'dzin 
11a5(kha): 'gag/ gnyis med rtogs pas mya ngan 'das/ yang dag lhun grub 'bras bu smin/ zhes gsungs so// nyon mongs rang grol ye shes 'khyel pa'i rgyud las/ 'bras bu rang grol du 
11a6(kha): bstan pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// // ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ bon nyid mi 'gyur spros bral dkyil 'khor nas/ rang byung ye shes 'gyur med 'di ru gsal/ mi gsal / 
11b1(kha): gsal ba'i bdag nyid can/ bdag phyogs bral ba'i byang chub sku/ tshen gang 'od kyi kun tu khyab/ rang gsal mnyam nyid con sku la/ rgyan dang cha lugs mtshan dpe longs spyod 
11b2(kha): s+dzogs/ mnyam la ma 'dras srul pa'i sku/ ngo bo yid bzhin nor bu nyid/ sku lnga mthar byin bade gshegs lnga/ gzhen lha rig pa'i snying po nyid/ ma pa thugs kyi dbyings chen te/ 
11b3(kha): khri khug dngos med mkha' yi sku/ yi srid yon tan bdal pa'i pbya/ mkha' 'gying mdzad spyod rnam par dag/ gnas 'dzin smra bsam rang bzhin med/ dbyings kyi cho 'drul thugs 
11b4(kha): rje shar/ lha lngas 'dzin pa'i zhen pa grol/ klong nas sprul pa'i lha dang gss/ gsas rje kun 'byung chen po'i klong / rgod gsas thugs rje chags med klong / gnam gss kun 
11b5(kha): sprul chen po'i glong / gar gsas mngon sul chen po'i glong / gnhen rab mtshan med dag pa'i gling / klong gi tsho 'dul regs lnga'i gss/ rigs lngar 'dzin pa'i rtog pa grol/ 
11b6(kha): b+ha ga'i klong chen yangs pa nas/ 'byung ba rnam lnga'i sprul pa shar/ mtshan med dag pa'i gnas 'gyur ba'i/ mkha' lngar sprul pa'i yum chen rnams/ byin rlabs bag ldan klong 
12a1(kha): nas shar/ yum du 'dzin pa'i chags pa grol/ cer gsal mkha' la sprul pa'i rtsal/ yi ghen ye sman 'dul ba'i ghein/ cer snang ye shes nyid la byung / 
12a2(kha): yod pa 'dzin pa'i chags pa grol/ brtson 'grus mthar pbyin sprul pa'i rtsal/ dus gsum ston pa gtsug pud gzhen/ sgo ba yab sum lasogs te/ dkyil 'khor phyag rgya 
12a3(kha): zhi ba'i lha/ rang las byung zhing rang las grol/ 'dul chen zhi ba'i lha tshogs rnams/ mkha' klong dbyings kyi cho 'phrul yin/ snang la dngos med gzha' tchen lta bu'i tshul/ sku 
12a4(kha): mdog phyag mtshan me long 'di bzhin gsal/ rgyan dang cha lugs chu zlo' dkyil 'khor s+dzogs/ skye ba med las skye ba'i cho 'phrul du / log rtog 'gro 'dul sku ru bstan pa 
12a5(kha): yang / 'dzin pa'i yul med bzung ba'i mtha' las grol/ s+dzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mkhyen pa'i ye zhes dang / mdzad pa'i 'phren las gsum du sprul pa yang / s+dzogs pa'i sangs 
12a6(kha): rgyas bder gshegs rigs lnga nyid/ thugs rje byin brlabs rgyud lnga'i sems can la/ ci ltar 'tshams pa bzhin du 'gro don mdzad/ mkhyen pa'i ye shes dri med ye shes lngas// 
12b1(kha): thugs rjes byin brlabs 'gro don s+dzogs par mdzad/ rang byung bon gsum thabs kyi khyad par ni/ ye zhes sgyu mar snang zhing gang ma yin/ ma sangs kun spyod ci la mi gnas shing / 
12b2(kha): don dam rgya mtsho nam mkha'i rgigs lthar dag/ ting 'dzin bye brag thabs kyi cho 'bhrul las/ 'byung basraim brtsegs dkyil 'khor ci snang ba/ ye zhes mkha' yang bha ga'i glong du 
12b3(kha): grol/ gzhal yas yid bzhin lhun gyis grub pa yang / skyon med yon tan phun sum 'tshogs ldan te/ che ba'i yon tan rnam dag mkha' la grol/ 'od zer sna tshogs 
12b4(kha): phyogs bcur 'phro ba yang / stong gsum 'jig rten khengs pa'i thugs rje ldan/ thugs rje chen po'i phyogs med yongs su grol/ rin chen khri rkang phyogs bzhi gsal ba yang / 
12b5(kha): bder gshegs dkyil 'khor 'dags pa'i bathu ldan zhing / bdud bzhi 'dul ba'i phyag rgya chen por grol/ seng ge glang chen nya dang zmag bya dang / shang sgang ma haM la sogs khri rnams kyang / 
12b6(kha): mi 'jigs stobs mchog s+dzu 'phrul rkang pa dbang / thar pa mya ngan 'das pa grol ba'i lam/ che ba'i yon tan gzhan las dpag pa'i phyir/ theg pa'i nang nas rgyal po lta bu ste// 
13a1(kha): y/ thabs kyis 'dul ba'i phyag rgya chen po grol/ parma mdzes pa'i 'di du 'bar ba yang / nyes pa'i skyon bral yon tan pun sum 'tshigs/ sna tshigs 'byung ba skye ba / 
13a2(kha): bzhi sgo khag/ rnam dag yon tan chen po'i phyag rgya grol/ rien chen nyi zla 'd du snang ba yang / 'jig rtyen yongs su sgron mar snang ba dang / ston gsum mun nag sel ba'i 
13a3(kha): mthu ldan pas/ yab yum gnyis med byang chub sems su grol/ 'gyur med gsung drung phyag rgya'i sku gsal ba/ 'gro 'dul dkyil 'khor bsam gyis mi khyab kyang / bde 
13a4(kha): gshegs rnams kyi thugs kyi dngos gzhi ste/ gcig las 'dod dgur bsgyur ba'i thugs rje che/ phyogs med zhing khams thabs kyi phyag rgya grol/ rgyan dang cha lugs mdzes pa sna / 
13a5(kha): tshogs kun/ yon tan rgyan gyis gdul bya r re 'dzoms/ dngos su ma grub chu zlo' dkyil 'khor bzhin/ cho 'drul thabs kyi phyag rgya chen por grol/ 'phen dang zar tshags 
13a6(kha): dang rgyal mtshan dang / bla re gdugs la sogs pa bsam mi khyab/ bon gyi ru mtshon dbyings la pyar la sogs/ bdud bzhi mgo bsnyal ngan song rnying mnan nas/ gdul bya'i 
13b1(kha): gnyen po gzhan las khyad par 'phags/ pha rol zil gyis gnon pa'i mthu ldan pas/ bon nyid klong na ril pa chen por grol/ phyag rgya chen po gcig tu ma nges shing / gsas 
13b2(kha): mkhar dbyings nas sprul pa'i cho 'dhrul 'gyed/ 'khor dang sprul pa yang sprul bcas pa'i tshogs/ bdag nyid sku gsung thugs las ma g.yis zhing / log rtig 'dul pbyir rnam pa 
13b3(kha): sna tshogs 'drul/ mkha' grong dbyings kyi cho 'drul chen por grol/ mi rtog spros bral mya ngan 'das pa dag/ 'das pa'i bon la bshad cing brtsal du med/ grol ba gsas mkhar 
13b4(kha): mi nub rgyal mtshan che/ che'i yangs pa bade chen lhun gyis grub/ ces gsungs so// nyon mongs rang grol ye shes 'khyel pa'i rgyud las/ zhi ba'i dkyil 'khor rang grol du 
13b5(kha): bstan pa'i le'u ste brgyad pa'o// / ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ ma byung ma g.yos thugs mchog las/ srid pa'i snying po yig 'bru mchog/ mtha' dbus med pa'i / 
13b6(kha): nam mkha' la/ thugs rje dbyings su dag pa'i a/ a las oM du gsal bar grub/ yi ge oM gyi snying po las/ mtshan med kun stong dag pa'i dbyings/ thugs rje chen po'i 
14a1(kha): h/ byin brlabs las/ ma g.yos ye nas 'du 'bral med/ thub pa med pa'i rgyal mtshan che/ ma panrg dbyings chen sku ru grub/ dug gsum mtshan med rang dg tu/ 
14a2(kha): s+dzogs sku mtshan pa'i ye shes dang / mdzad pa'i 'phrin las dag par grol/ thugs nyid ma g.yos dgongs pa yi/ rang grol zhi ba'i mi 'dul ba/ mkha' klong dbyings kyi cho 'hrul 
14a3(kha): du / gsas mkhar mi nub stong pa nyid/ ma parg dbyings chen thugs ka nas/ reg pa 'drel ba'i yi ge a/ 'od dpung nag po ram gyi 'od/ mi tnhub rgyal mtshan phyag rgya che/ 
14a4(kha): bskyed pa'i sngags kyis bskul pa las/ khro mchog 'brug gsas tchem pa dang / srid pa'i sa bdag stong khyab ma/ mthing nag 'jigs pa'i cha lugs kyis/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor 
14a5(kha): gdan la bzhugs/ sa bdag gsang ba lag chen dang / sred pa'i bdud chen sor nyag la/ 'jigs pa'i cha lugs khros tshul ston/ srid pa stong gsum 'jig rten pa/ ra grags 
14a6(kha): gdangs kyi khros pa'i skling / nyon mongs gti mug 'thebs pa la/ ma g.yois spros bral dbyings nas khrol/ gdangs skad zil gnon zhugs chen 'byug/ skye 'jig don la 'gyur 
14b1(kha): med gsas/ las dang nyon mongs dbyings nas 'cham/ srid pa'i 'jig rten sa yi bdag/ stong gsum b+ha ga'i klong gis khyab/ skye 'gro kun gyi yum 'gyur ma/ thabs dang shes rab / 
14b2(kha): gnyis med las/ lhag pa gsung dung sems 'phres pas/ gti mug gnas dag 'dzoms pa'i phag/ nyon mongs gting len chu drin gdong / dbu gsum dbang drag zhi bar ston/ 
14b3(kha): thugs ni ma g.yis gsal bar gnas/ phyag dug brlag pa'i 'phrin las mdzod/ zhabs ni mi 'tchor dbyings su 'dabs/ gti mug rnam dag ma g.yis klong / mtshan med rang 
14b4(kha): byung chen por grol/ zhes gsungs so// nyon mongs rang grol ye shes 'khyil pa'i rgyud las/ 'brug gsas chem pa rang grol du bstan pa'i le'u ste dgu pa'o// // de nas ston pa'i 
14b5(kha): sgrin mas bka' stsal pa/ rang byung ye shes mi 'gyur thugs nyid la/ sred pa'i snying po yig 'bru mchog/ rig pa shar ba'i nam mkha' la/ 'gyur med dbyings su dag pa'i a/ 
14b6(kha): ma skyes a las oM du grub/ yi ge oM gyi 'od zer las/ srid pa gdar gcod dag pa'i dbyings/ gdod nas skye 'gag gnyis su med/ bon nyid klong nas longs spyod s+dzogs/ gsal / 
15a1(kha): @/ la rig pa'i phyag rgya che/ ghen lha dkar po'i sku ru grub/ dug gsum 'khor ba gting dag tu/ gsal ba'i sku dang mkhyen pa'i mdzod/ mdzad pa'i 'phren las rnam / 
15a2(kha): dag cing / mtshan med sgyu 'prul phyag rgya grol/ thugs nyid 'gyur med dgongs pa yis/ rang grol zhi bas mi 'dul la/ mkha' glong dbyings kyi cho 'drul du/ gsas mkhar dag 
15a3(kha): pa kun gsal nyid/ gnhin lha dkar po'i thugs ka nas/ skar chen 'dra ba'i yi ge kha/ 'od dpung dkar po ram gyi 'od/ mi 'gyur g.yung drung 'od du gsal/ bskyed pa'i sngags kyi 
15a4(kha): bar snang la/ khro ba khra gsas khyung rgod dang / khro mo sred pa'i kha 'bar ma/ dkar mo 'jzigs pa'i cha lugs kyis/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gdan la bzhugs/ bdud nag sbung ngnag 
15a5(kha): po dang / dri za log pa'i nyams sod len/ 'jigs byed mkha' la khros tshul ston/ shar phyogs srid pa'i 'jig rten du/ srid pa'i klong nas gsung dbyangs khrod/ nyon mongs zhe sdang 
15a6(kha): 'bar ba la/ ma bcos 'gyur med dbyings nas 'khro/ nyon mongs mi 'chor dpungs 'djoms khra/ sprul pa phyogs med 'gyed pa'i gsas/ thugs rjes spyi rgya gcod pa'i khyung / kun 
15b1(kha): gyi yang drud gyur pa'i rgod/ sab dang cha lugs mthun pa'i hra/ chags med kling dag lha mo'i dbyings/ kha nas mi 'bar dus mtha' bsreg/ thabs dang shes rab gnyis med las// / 
15b2(kha): lhag pa'i gsung dung sems 'phres pas/ zhe sdang ro bi 'dzoms pa'i sang / nyon mongs khog 'og chud pa'i rgod/ dbu gsum dbang srag zhi bar ston/ thugs nyid mi 'gyur byams par 
15b3(kha): gnas/ phyag dug sred pa'i pur bu 'drel/ zhabs ni srid pa'i dbyings su 'dabs/ zhe sdang zhing dag 'gyur med klong / gdar gcod rang byung chen por grol/ zhes gsungs so// nyon 
15b4(kha): mongs rang grol ye shes 'khyil pa'i rgyud las/ khra gsas yab yum rang grol du bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu pa'o// // ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ rang byung rang bzhin med 
15b5(kha): pa las/ sred pa'i snying po yi ge mcshig/ thugs je ltos pa'i nam mkha' la/ 'dod dgu dbyings su dag pa'i a/ skye med a las o dugyur/ yi ge o gyi byin brlabs las/ 
15b6(kha): yon tan 'dod dgur dag pa'i dbyings/ khri kzhug rgyal po'i sku ru grub/ dug gsum nyon mongs gting dag tu/ rang bzhin sku la cho 'phrul rgyan/ 'phrin las che yang rnam par dag/ 
16a1(kha): yoMn tan zhing dag phyag rgyaur grol/ 'gyur ba med pa'i phyag rgya che/ rang bzhin dbyings su dag pa'i thugs/ mnyam nyid chen po'i dgongs pa yis/ rang grol zhi bas 
16a2(kha): mi 'dul la/ mkha' glong dbyings kyi cho 'drul du/ gsas mkhar kun snyoms mnyam pa nyid/ khri khug rgyal po'i thugs ka nas/ 'od pung 'dus pa'i yi g ta/ 'd pung sdug 
16a3(kha): poer ram gyi 'od/ rin chen 'bar ba'i 'od du gsal/ bskyed pa'i sngags kyis mnyam nyid du/ khro bo ma gsas kham nag dang / khro mo sred pa'i dza la ma/ skug nag 'jigs pa'i 
16a4(kha): cha lugs kyis/ nye ma'i dkyil 'khor gdan la bzhugs/ gzhin rje'i dmyal ba'i thig 'debs dang / gnhin rje 'chi bdag nag po la/ 'jigs byed chen po'i khros tshul ston/ 
16a5(kha): lho phyogs srid pa'i 'jig rten du/ 'bar ba'i klong nas gsung dbyangs 'gro/ nyon mongs nga rgyal sphrin pung la/ rang bzhin med pa'i dbyings nas 'khro/ ye shes mae dpung nyon mongs 
16a6(kha): bsregs/ byin rlabs cir yang gsal ba'i gsas/ dbang drag mkha' la brjid pa'i khams/ dus gsum 'gyur ba med pas nag/ rgyan dang cha lugs yab bzhin khro/ snang srid / 
16b1(kha): 'jig rten dbang sdud ma/ srid gsum 'jig rten sgrol ba'i dza/ las dang thugs rjes 'brel ba la/ kun gyi gzhi ru gyur pa'i ma/ thabs dang shes rab gnyis med las/ lhag pa'i / 
16b2(kha): g.sung drung sems 'phros pas/ nga rgyal gting nas 'dzoms pa'i stag/ nyon mongs zhing nas sgrol ba'i 'ug/ dbu gsum dbang drag zhi bar ston/ thugs ni rang bzhin mnyam nyid 
16b3(kha): gnas/ phyag dug srid pa gting nas 'djoms/ zhabs ni dbang sud dbyings su dag/ nga rgyal rang dag rang bzhin glong / gting dag rang byung chen por grol/ zhes gsungs so// nyon mongs 
16b4(kha): rang grol ye zhes 'khyil pa'i rgyud las/ me gsas yab yum rang grol du bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu gcig pa'o// / ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ rang byung mtshan med 
16b5(kha): dag pa las/ ma chags thabs kyi sa bon du/ srid pa 'dus pa'i snying po mchog/ bag chags nub pa'i nam mkha' la/ 'od dkar 'drel ba'i klong nyid du/ stobs mchog dbang du 
16b6(kha): gyur pa'i/ 'gag med a las oM du grub/ yi ge oM gyi 'phro 'du las/ dbang chen kun khyab srid pa'i dbyings/ ye nas bzang ngan dus mtha' med/ ci snang ci srid rol pa'i rgyan/ 
17a1(kha): tag pa b'gyur yon tan che/ ye srid bya chen sku ru grub/ dug gsum bag chags ye dag tu/ s+dzogs pa'i sku la yon tan mchog/ stobs kyi rgyal po lhun 
17a2(kha): gyis grub/ dbang chen 'byams yas phyag rgyar grol/ chags med mtha' bral dgongs pa yis/ zhi ba'i thabs kyis mi 'dul la/ mkha' klong dbyings kyi cho 'drul du / gsas / 
17a3(kha): mkhar sor rtogs chags med dbyings/ ye srid pbya chen thugs ka nas/ me dpung 'drel ba'i yi ge tsha/ 'odi dpung le brgan ram gyi 'od/ dri med pa r+ga'i snying por gsal/ bskyed pa 
17a4(kha): sngags kyi nam mkha' la/ khro ba dbal gsas me 'bar dang / khro mo sred pa'i 'di 'phro ma/ dmar nag 'jigs pa'i cha lugs kyis/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gdan la bzhugs/ 
17a5(kha): klu bdu mer ba 'khyiel chen dang / gtan dmar khro boa blang mg la/ brjed pa'i sku yi khro tshul ston/ bub phyogs sred pa'i 'jig rten du/ stobs mtshog glong nas khros pa'i 
17a6(kha): gdangs/ nyon mongs 'dod chags tsha 'gyu ma/ chags med dag pa'i dbyings nas 'khro/ thugs rje mthu stobs sprul pa'i dbal/ bag chags gnas su dag pa'i gsas/ snang srid 
17b1(kha): gting nas sreg pa'i me/ mtshan med dag pa'i klong du 'bar/ mthu stobs yab dang mnyam par khro/ srid pa 'jig rten las la sgrol/ ye zhes sprul pa thugs kyi 'odi/ phyogs bcu / 
17b2(kha): kun du bdag med 'phro/ mnyam rig stobs su gyur pa'i ma/ thabs dang zhes rab gnyis med pas/ lhag pa'i gsung drung sems 'phres pa/ 'dod chags thabs mkhas gteing nas len/ 
17b3(kha): byei la pa hud chags sdang 'dzoms/ dbu gsum dbang drag znhi bar ston/ thugs ni chags med sbyin pa'i glong / phyag dug seid pa mkha' la bsgyur/ nabs ni chags med dbyings su 
17b4(kha): 'debs/ 'dod chags bral ba chags med kling / 'dod chags rang byung chen por grol/ zhes gsungs so// nyon mongs rang grol ye shes 'khyil pa'i rgyud las/ dbal gsas yab 
17b5(kha): sum rang grol du bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu gnyis pa'o// / ston pa'i sgron mas bka' rtsal pa/ rang byung mtshan med dag pa las/ sred pa'i bcud bsdus yi ge mchog/ sgrib pa 
17b6(kha): sbyang ba'i nam mkha' la/ rtsal med dbyings su dag pa'i a/ dag pa'i a las oM du grub/ yi ge oM gyi 'phro 'du las/ byin brlabs phun sum 'tshogs pa'i dbyings/ mkha' 
18a1(kha): @/ 'gying dkar po'i sku ru grub/ dug gsum mtshan med gting len du/ gzi byin dbang stobs phyag rgya che/ rnam par grol ba'i byin brlabs mchog/ rtsal med sku 
18a2(kha): la yon tan zhing / 'phrin las dag pa rnam grol rgyan/ mtshan ma med pa'i dgongs pa yis/ zhi ba'i phyag rgya ma 'dul la/ mkha' klong dbyings kyi cho 'bhrul du/ gsas mkhar 
18a3(kha): brtsal med nan tan dbyings/ mkha' 'gying brjod pa'i thugs ka nas/ gser mdog snying po yi ges/ 'di dpung ser po ram gyi 'od/ glog dmar 'khyug pa'i ral gri gsal/ 
18a4(kha): bskyed pa'i sngags kyis mkha' gsal la/ khro bo glog gsas 'odi 'gyu dang / khro mo sred pa'i me 'gyu ma/ ser nag 'jigs pa'i cha lugs kyi/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gdan la 
18a5(kha): bzhugs/ gnod sbyin ha la gdng brgyad dang / bgegs chen byi na ya ka la/ gzi brjid chen po'i khros tshul ston/ byang phyogs srid pa'i 'jig rten du/ gzi byin gdangs kyi 
18a6(kha): klong nas 'khro/ nyon mongs phrag dag 'tshubs pa la/ mtshan med grol ba'i dbyings nas 'khro/ brtson 'grus stobs hugs glog bas myur/ mkha' klong gnyis su ma sgrib gsal/ 
18b1(kha): phyi nang med par thugs rje'i 'di/ 'gro don mthar phyin s+dzogs par 'gyur/ yab dang cha lugs srid par khri/ me lces las dang bag chags sreg/ 'gyu ba thugs rjes sems can la/ 
18b2(kha): byams mgon ma ltar khyab pa'i ma/ thabs dang shes rab gnyis med las/ lhag pa'i g.yung dung sems 'phros pas/ phrag dog gting len 'dzoms pa'i drid/ bslu byed thabs mkhas 
18b3(kha): pa khang mgo/ dbu gsum dbang drag zhi bar ston/ thugs ni bsam med mtha' las 'das/ phyag drug srid pa gting nas len/ zhabs ni rtsal med dbyings su 'debs/ phrag dog 
18b4(kha): mtshan med yangs pa'i glong / rang byung chen pos dbyings su grol/ rnam dag rtsal med cig le tshe/ zhes gsungs so// nyon mongs rang grol ye shes 'khyil pa'i rgyud las/ glog 
18b5(kha): gsas yab sum rang grol du bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu gsum pa'o// / ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ rang byung ye shes mkhyen pa las/ snang sred 'dus pa'i yi ge ru/ 
18b6(kha): dgongs pa ye shes nam mkha' la/ 'dul ba'i thugs rje'i yi ge bso/ dag pa thugs rjes 'od zer 'phro/ rig pa dbyings su 'dus pa las/ 'du 'phro cho 'phul byin rlabs klong / 
19a1(kha): / rkye 'gags gnyis md rnam par dag/ gdug pa 'dal mzad kun gyi re/ gs je dg pa'i rku ru g la/ nyon mongs mtshan bed gting len du/ byen rlabs ra 
19a2(kha): la gzi brjid gsang / dri med thugs gsal che ba'i rgyan/ brtsal med lhun grub s+dzogs sangs rgyas/ thugs rje chen po'i phyag rgyar grol/ thugs rje rnam dag dgongs pa yi// 
19a3(kha): zhe ba'i thabs kyis mi 'dul la/ mkha' glong dbyings kyi cho 'brul du/ gsas mkhar thugs je reg pa'i kling / gsas rje gsal ba'i thugs ka nas/ rig pa gsal ba'i yi ge 
19a4(kha): b/ 'od dpung sngo skya riam gyi 'od/ rig pa 'drel ba'i lhags kyur gsal/ chu la nya ldang tshul bzhin du/ khro ba mkha' 'gying chen po dang / khro mo sred pa'i gtum klong ma/ sngo skya / 
19a5(kha): 'jigs pa'i cha lugs kyi/ nye ma'i dkyil 'khor gdan la bzhugs/ me 'brung drang srong po ma la/ brjid pa'i cha lugs zhin du 'khro/ shar lho sred pa'i 'jig rten du/ gsung gi 
19a6(kha): tshams ngam drag por 'khro/ log 'dren chu ltar g.yo ba la/ rig pa'i ye shes dbyings nas 'phro/ bon nyid rnam dag mkha' gsal la/ rig pa'i ye shes brjid 'gyeing ba/ mi 
19b1(kha): g.yo mnyam pa'i dbyings chen po/ hin tu 'jigs pa'i tshul gyis khro/ phyin ci log dgu'i zhad gcod gtum/ con nyid mi g.yo bde chen kling / yongs la khyab bdag kun / 
19b2(kha): 'byung ma/ thabs dang shes rab gnyis med las/ lhag pa gsung drung sems 'phres pa/ log 'khrul shes pa gcod pa'i dam/ rig pa'i gnas 'debs po rig mgo/ dbu gsum dbang 
19b3(kha): drag zhi bar ston/ thugs nyid rig pa dag pa'i krlong / phyag dug log 'dren dgra bgegs 'dul/ nabs ni thugs rjes dbyings su 'dabs/ log 'dran skyon med thugs rje glong / rang 
19b4(kha): byung skye med dbyings su grol/ mtshan med dngos dag mkha' ltar yangs/ zhes gsungs so// nyon mongs rang grol ye shes 'khyel pa'i rgyud las/ mkha' 'gying yab yum rang grol du 
19b5(kha): bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu bzhi pa'o// / ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ rang byung ye shes zhan med las/ gdug pa 'dzoms pa'i yi ge ru/ thugs nyid ye shes nam 
19b6(kha): mkha' la/ bsam dag thugs rje'i yi ge bso/ zhen med thugs rjes 'od zer 'phro/ byin brlabs dbyings su 'dus pa las/ 'du 'phro cho 'phrul kun grol klong / gting nas

22a1(kha): dbyengs kyi nam mkha' la/ gnas du dag pa'i yi ge ba'o/ rtog med ye zhes 'di zer 'dro/ 'tkhor ba gteng dag dbyings su 'das/ 'dg 'pro sbyor ba'i tshoe 'dul blong /

22b1(kha): byed mkha' la 'gro/ byang kar sred pa'i 'jig ten du/ klong nas lu tshem dr gzhul 'gro/ shin d gdg cing rigs pa la/ ceng med zhe ba'i dbyings nas 'gro/ phyag rgya chen po /

36b3(kha): sgrol byed gze ma bcu ru gsal/ lag g.yas haM la yab yum bsgom/ lag g.yon hu la yab yum bsgom/ rkang g.yas ho la yab yum bsgom/ de ltar gsal 'dres / 
36b4(kha): goms pa yis/ lha sku phyag rgya chen po ste/ rang lus dkyil 'khor chen po s+dzogs/ gdes pa can gyi phung po grol/ bsnyen pa'i dus sam yang na ni/ phal cher rtsa ba'i lha 
36b5(kha): rnams bsgom/ phyag rgya chen po'i sa chen gnon/ sgrub dus sung ma bkod pa bkyi/ bdag gi spyan mig g.yas g.yon gnyis/ khra gss khyung rgod thabs kyi bya/ khyung sman sung 
36b6(kha): gshog shes rab yum/ dbu yi gnas lngar gsang khra lnga/ dbu skra ljang lo grangs med la/ khra yi sprul pa 'bum tshogs bsgom/ lhag rus dang ni 'jug rus la/ rin chen gdug 
37a1(kha): pa'i gcan spyang dang / bdang ldan 'd kye bra lnga bsgom/ tshigs chen bzhe dang nte ras la/ gcan spyang gdug pa lnga rnams bsgom/ sgal tshigs rtsib gur thams / 
37a2(kha): cad kun/ khra syang sprul pa'i tshogs su bsgom/ gsang bsdin chen 'byung gnas la/ sa bdag tsa tsang 'khor ba dang / stong khyab brtyan ma gser mdog bsgom/ glo snying mkhal ma 
37a3(kha): pho 'cher la/ sa bdag chen po lnga ru bsgom/ nang grol khrag dang chu ser tshogs/ sa bdag spul pa 'byum tshogs bsgom/ de ltar bsgom zhing las la thad/ shin du gsal zhing 
37a4(kha): brtan par/ nye ba'i snying po 'di 'drel ltar/ kun gnhi mi g.yo dbyings su thim/ rtogs pa rang lus gting nas grol/ grub na gzhan rgyud log pa rnams/ byin brlabs thabs 
37a5(kha): kyis bsgral ba'i phyir/ bdag gi ba pu' bu gkun/ las mkhan po mo bsam mi khyab/ rgya bye'u gtams pa ltar du gnas/ bdag nyid gtso bo'i stobs kyi bthas/ 'jig ten 
37a6(kha): khrengs pa'i dmag tu langs/ gzas pa pho mo'i tshe bkrag bsdus/ gzugs phung thal bar brlag par bya/ rnam zhes 'od kyi thig le de/ rin chen phur pa'i rtsi la dril/ bdag nyid 
37b1(kha): gtso ba'i thugs kar bsdus/ thig le byang chub sems su zhu/ spros med byang chub sems su thim/ grub pa'i gzhan rgyud mkha' la grol/ zhes gsungs so// nyon mongs rang 
37b2(kha): grol ye zhes 'khyil pa'i rgyud las/ gdos pa dang bcas pa'i phung po rang grol du bstan pa'i le'u ste nyi shu drug pa'o// // ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ bye brag ming gis 
37b3(kha): bsdus pa'i bon/ thams cad de bzhin nyid la 'dus/ yongs su khyab cing bdal par gnas/ byin brlabs 'dus pa'i cho 'phrul las/ dug lnga rtsad gcod 'dul ba'i lha/ mi bzad 
37b4(kha): drag po dbal bur sku/ gsang gnas 'khor lo 'byung ba dang / tcig le gnas 'gyur ngo sprod pa/ thugs ka gsang ba bye tshangs gnas/ con nyid dbyings kyi 'khor lo'i dbus/ sna 
37b5(kha): tshogs 'drel ba ye shes 'od/ 'byung ba 'dus pa'i dang ma la/ dbal chen mkha' 'gying bdud 'dul dang / stong khyab dbyings kyi rgyal mo gnyis/ 'khrel byor gnyis med rgyan rnams 
37b6(kha): s+dzogs/ nas 'bru tsam du bskyed cing 'god/ 'byung bzlung gi dang ma ste/ rang byung mkhyen pa'i ye shes yin/ rang 'byung ye shes cig le'i mchog/ sna tshogs 'brel ba ye shes rtsa/ 
38a1(kha): de las srog 'dzin rtsa lngar gyis/ rtsa sblab rnam shes rgyu ba'bung / dngas ma 'byung ba chen po lnga/ bcud las ye shes lnga ru gsal/ shar phyogs dara skud 'dra ba'i rtsa/ 
38a2(kha): mi 'gyur cig le chen po la/ khro ba khra gss khyung rgod dang / khro mo kha 'bar yum chen gnyis/ 'khrel sbyor cha 'pha rgyan rnams s+dzogs/ nas 'bru tsam du bskyed cing dgod/ 
38a3(kha): 'byung ba sa yi dngas ma ste/ me long lta bu ye shes yin/ lho phyogs mu tig 'dra ba'i rtsa/ yon tan 'od kyi thig le la/ khro bo ma gsas khams nag dang / khro ba yum chen dza 
38a4(kha): la ma/ 'khril sbyor cha phra rgyan rnams s+dzogs/ nas 'bru tsam du bskyed cing dgod/ 'byung ba chu'i dngas ma ste/ mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes yin/ nhub phyogs nyi zer 'dra ba'i rtsa/ 
38a5(kha): dbang mchog 'od kyi thig le la/ khro ba dbal gsas me 'bar dang / yum chen khro mo 'di 'phro ma/ 'khril sbyor cha 'phra rgyan rnams s+dzogs/ nas 'bru tsam du bskyed cing dgod/ 
38a6(kha): 'byung ba me yi dngs ma ste/ so sor rtogs pa'i ye zshes yin/ byang phyogs gser gyi ba thag tsalas grub 'od kyi thig le la/ khro bo glog gsas 'di 'gyu dang / khro ma yum chen 
38b1(kha): me 'gyu ma/ 'khrel sbyr cha phra rgyan rnams s+dzogs/ nas 'bru tsam du bskyed cing bsgom/ 'byung bslung gi dangas ma ste/ bya ba nan tan ye shes yin/ steng phyogs gzha' tshen dar 
38b2(kha): skud rtsa/ brtsal med 'od kyi thig le la/ dbal chen stag la me 'bar dang / sum chen thugs rje byams ma gnyis/ 'khrel byor cha sra rgyan rnams s+dzogs/ nas 'bru tsam du 
38b3(kha): bskyed cing dgod/ 'byung ba nam mkha'i dangas ma ste/ stong pa nyid kyi ye shes yin/ de ltar rtsa lnga'i byin rlabs las/ phyi rol yul gyi 'byung ba lnga/ sha khrag drid dbugs rnam shes 
38b4(kha): lnga/ bsnyen pa ye shes chig le lnga/ mi rtag dug lnga'i sa bon yin/ khong stong tchig le byang chub sems/ de yi phyi rim rtsa chen bzhi/ kha dag dbyibs dang ldan par gnas/ de ltar 
38b5(kha): rtsa chen brgyad po d/ kun gzhi rnam zshes brgyad kyi rtsa/ khongs steng phyogs byang sems rtsa/ lho shar dkar 'khyil dung gi rtsa/ 'd dpung 'khyil ba'i rtsa mdud du/ khro ba mkha' 
38b6(kha): 'gying gyad chen dang / khro mo sred pa'i gtum klong gnyis/ rgyan s+dzogs dod mdzes phra mor bsgom/ lho nub skug po pa khang rtsa/ 'od dpung 'khyil ba'i rtsa mdud du / khro ba bdud nag 
39a1(kha): @/ 'bar ba dang / khro mo sred pa'i dba' klong gnyis/ rgyan s+dzogs dod mdzes phra mor bsgom/ nub byang dmar ser zla gam rtsa/ 'd dpung 'khyil pa'i rtsa mdud du/ khro bo / 
39a2(kha): gnam grag pa chen dang / khro mo sred pa'i sgra 'byin gnyis/ rgyan s+dzogs dod mzes pra mor bsgom/ byang shar gu gsum ldang ser rtsa/ 'd dpung 'khyil ba'i rtsa mdud du/ khro ba / 
39a3(kha): sdom chen 'khyil pa dang / khro mo srid pa'i ral ka gnyis/ rgyan s+dzogs dod mdzes phra mor bsgom/ yon tan mtha' yi rtsa bzhi la/ sgo ba yab yum brgyad rnams bsgom/ phyi / 
39a4(kha): rol su ris nyi shu la/ khra thabs gze ma nyi shu bsgom/ thugs ka gsang ba'i bye' tshang gi/ she thun mang kher gur khang dbus/ kun gzhi 'od kyi khang pa na/ rtsa ba'i lha rnams 
39a5(kha): s+dzogs par gnas/ de la yid 'dres goms brtan na/ nyon mongs yid kyi rnam zhes grol/ ye shes blo yis sa chen gnon/ phyi gtsug cags phyug mo' gnas/ rtsa 'dab rgyas 
39a6(kha): pa'i lte dbus na/ khra gsas khyung sman yab yum gnyis/ rtsa 'dab rnams la gsang khra'i tshogs/ mgrin pa sdug bsngal kun 'dzom gnas/ rtsa 'dab rgyas pa'i lte dbus na// 
39b1(kha): rin chen gcan spyang yab yum la/ rtsa 'dab rnams la khra spyang tshogs/ lte ba srid pa bskyed pa'i gnas/ rtsa 'dab rgyas pa'i lte dbus na/ rtsang rtsang 'khor ba yab yum gnyis// 
39b2(kha): lhag ma'i rtsa 'dab byi ma la/ sa bdag mtsho sman spul pa'i tshogs/ gsang ba b+ha gkun bskyed gnas/ rtsa 'dab rgyas pa'i lte dbus na/ thugs je byams ma ni khro gnyis/ 
39b3(kha): rtsa 'dab phyi ma rnams la yang / yid sems kha sdud bud med rnams/ rkang pa blung gi 'khor lo la/ las mkhan phyi ma thams cad bskyed/ de rnams sprul pa las sbyor dus/ gnas 
39b4(kha): nas sprul zhing mkha' la bkyi/ gang la bya ba'i dngos po rnams/ skad cig tsam yang mi gnas par/ che srog phur pa'i rtse la bsdus/ pur rtsi gtso ba'i thugs kar stim/ de 
39b5(kha): gsum mi pyed gcig gingan/ bon nyid sems kyi thig ler 'dus/ skye med byang chub sems su grol/ gsal stong 'gyur med mi tnub cshe/ bdag gzhan rgyud sgrol thabs kyi 
39b6(kha): mchog/ bde chen gsang ba'i skur thob 'gyur/ zhes gsungs so// nyon mongs rang grol ye shes 'khyil pa'i rgyud las/ rtsa dang thig le gsang gnas rang grol du bstan pa'i le'u ste 
40a1(kha): nye shu bdun pa'o// / ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ ma byas bon nyid ye sred la/ rol pa'i rtsal du ci shar yang / sna tshigs bon kun sems la 'dus/

40a5(kha): yang / gnas dag rang grol chen po nyid/ de bzhin khra gss yab sum kyang / gdul bya dru za po mo gnyis/ gnas 'gyur rnam shes phung po yais/ nyon mongs zhe sdang gnas su 
40a6(kha): dag/ me gsas kham pa yab yum gnyis/ gdul bya gshin rje pho mo la/ gnas 'gyur 'du byed phung po'o// nyon mongs nga rgyal gnas su dag/ dbal gsas me 'bar yab yum 
40b1(kha): gnyis/ gdul bya kru bdu po mo la/ gnas 'gyur tsher ba'i phung po'o// nyon mongs 'dod chags gnas du dag/ blog gsas 'di 'byung yab sum gnyis/ gdul bya gnod byin po / 
40b2(kha): mo la/ gnas 'gyur 'du shes phung po'// nyon mongs phrag dog gnas su dag/ sa chu m srlung nam mkha' la/ yum lnga gnas dag 'byung ba'i klong / mkha' 'gying gyad chen yab 
40b3(kha): yum gnyis/ gdul bya me lha pho mo dang / gnas 'gyur lus kyi dbang po'o// nyon mongs log 'dren gnas su dag/ bdud nag 'bar ba yab yum gnyis/ gdul bya srin po pho mo 
40b4(kha): la/ gnas 'gyur sna yi dbang po'o// nyon mongs gdug sems gnas su dag/ gnam grags par chen yab yum gnyis/ gdul bblung lha pho ma dang / gnas 'gyur rna ba'i pung 
40b5(kha): po'o// byung cher khyab 'jug gnas su dag/ sdom chen 'khyil pa yab yum gnyis/ gdul bya bdud dang gdan bral la/ gnas 'gyur le'i dbang po'// nyon mongs srigs pa gnas 
40b6(kha): su dag/ stag la me 'bar yab yum gnyis/ gdul bya bgegs dang srin po la/ gnas 'gyur mig gi dbang po'o// nyon mongs nga bdag gnas su dag/ gzugs sgra dri ro reg bya la/ 
41a1(kha): mtshams kyi yum lnga rnam par dag/ yid kyi rnam shes skye 'phel las/ nye shu nye ba'i nyon mongs rnams/ gze ma khra thabs nyi bu ru/ gnas dag mtshan ma med

41a3(kha): gdul bya thams cad dbang du 'dus/ phyi ma 'bras bu thob pa yang / yi ge 'khor lo tshogs chens/ che ba'i yon tan longs spyod rgyan/ 'bras bu zhing khams s+dzogs pa'i mchog/

41b6(kha): nub rgyal mtshan 'bras bu mchog/ rtag pa chen po 'gyur ba med/ mi 'gyur g.yung drung brnyan pa'i thugs/ dus gsum kun gyi rje ru gyur/ ma lus s+dzogs pa'i 'og men 
42a1(kha): @/ gnas/ rang 'byung bskal pa 'bras bu ltar/ dus su tsig mtha' med las byung / khri khug rgyal po rnam par dag/ me gsas kham nag che ba grol/ dza la dgyes pa'i / 
42a2(kha): po brang yang / che 'i yangs so mdud pa grol/ thams cad bkag pa gang yang med/ ye nas mi 'gyur g.sung drung dbyings/ bon nyid mi 'gyur bdal pa'i snying po che/ phyogs dang res med

42a4(kha): srid par shar/ yi bsrid bya chen rnam par dag/ dbal gsas me 'bar che ba grol/ 'di 'phro yum gyi bde klong yang / cho' yangs so mdud pa grol/ yum chen srid pa'i ba mo che/

43a1(kha): dbyings kyi sum nyid dang / 'byung ba mkha' ye sum nyid dang / gzung ma gsang ba'i sum nyid do// gzung ma kun bskyed bde sum la/ bde chen rgyan gyi dkyil 'tkhor /

43a5(kha): phyogs mtshams med par kun du rgyug/ grub pa med pa bya ba mang / gang la tshogs med kun rjes stog/ deyi don gsung 'di skad de// 'di lta bu'i khang dbus ni/ rin chen shel gyi /
